I stayed in a high-floor room. The room was big enough. There was a large floor-to-ceiling window in the room that could directly see the city view. Even Overlooking Taihu Lake. The room is fully equipped,
2. What impressed me most was the very good service in the hotel. Here are a few examples:
   (1) There are welcome fruits, snacks and milk every day. The service staff will greet you when you meet them when you go out, and the room is cleaned.
   (2) We, as a couple, love to drink tea, and we will bring our own tea sets and tea leaves when we travel. One day when we returned to the hotel from a trip, we found two small bottles of the local specialty Anji White Tea for us to taste.
   (3) It happens to be a consecutive holiday during breakfast, and there will be someone at the elevator entrance to guide the restaurant.
   (4) When we checked out on the last day of our stay, the receptionist knew that we were going to visit the Hubi Museum, and specially gave us a Hubi with the hotel‚Äôs name on it as a parting gift.
3. The breakfast attached to the hotel is very good. You can taste different Chinese and Western flavors. You only have one stomach, so you can't taste everything.
4. Overall, it is highly recommended and will be my first consideration next time I go to Huzhou.
5. The only disadvantage of the hotel is that the underground parking lot is shared with other buildings. When there are many people and people come back late, it often takes a lot of time to find a parking space. There is no dedicated area for customers to park conveniently. Moreover, every time the car needs to leave the underground parking lot, it takes a lot of time. You need to report your car number to the counter first, instead of reporting it once, you can show up on your own for free.

Although the brand of hand sanitizer is not the acca kappa white moss smell of other famous Kaiyuan cities, it tastes equally good. The mattresses and pillows in the bedroom are soft and comfortable. The front desk was given a north-facing position, which not only has a river view, but also can see the distant Taihu landmarks Sheraton, Xinglilan Hotel, and even Taihu Lake and Dongting Mountain in Suzhou. It's great! The TV is relatively old because the hotel opened in 2014, and it doesn't have a screen projection function. There's nothing we can do about it, it's not a big problem.
Sound insulation: The hotel elevator room is specially enclosed in an area, some distance away from the guest rooms, so there is no need to worry about being disturbed by the sound of the elevator door opening.
Breakfast: The hotel's breakfast dining area is large and the content is very rich. It has a variety of cold dishes, hot dishes, freshly cooked, black rice, tofu curd, five-spice dried tofu, etc., which surpasses most international five-star hotels. So much so that I was reluctant to leave and ate for an entire hour and a half! ! Lunch is skipped!
Service: The hotel service quality is first-class, which also reflects the style of the famous Kaiyuan capital. When checking in, the front desk gave us welcome fruits and mung bean cakes with the word "Delun" printed on them, which were very delicious. The hotel has more than 10 bottles of Nongfu Spring at the elevator entrance on each floor of the guest room for guests to take. Regarding the check-out time, the hotel is also very flexible and there is no mandatory requirement to check out before 12 o'clock. When checking out, the lady at the front desk also gave me a souvenir. The lady at the front desk was so pretty!
Summary: A perfect trip to the famous Kaiyuan capital. These four words, Kaiyuan capital, are worthy of being the number one brand of high-end hotel chains in China! I hope that the Kaiyuan name will spread all over the country!
